Psychiatrische Klinik am Klinikum Bremerhaven Reinkenheide soll mit einem Neubau ausgebaut und weiterentwickelt werden Dies teilt der Aufsichtsratsvorsitz des Klinikums Stadtrat Melf Grantz mit Die Klinik f r Psychiatrie und Psychotherapie am Klinikum Bremerhaven Reinkenheide sei seit Jahren berproportional ausgelastet und m sse dringend weiterentwickelt werden sagt Melf Grantz Eine Ausweitung der station ren Kapazit ten und Leistungsangebote ist von der zust ndigen Beh rde bereits genehmigt worden Da die r umliche Situation mittlerweile derart beengt sei und eine Sanierung des in den er Jahren gebauten Hauses w hrend des laufenden Betriebs nicht zumutbar sei habe der Aufsichtsrat beschlossen einen dreigeschossigen Erg nzungsbau errichten zu lassen um dann den bisherigen Klinikbau zu einem Funktionsbau umzugestalten Damit kann sich die Klinik f r Psychiatrie und Psychotherapie zu einem modernen Psychiatrischen Zentrum mit verbesserten therapeutischen M glichkeiten weiterentwickeln betont Stadtrat Melf Grantz Wie Grantz weiter erkl rt sei von einem Gutachten das der renommierte Psychiater Prof Peter Kruckenberg erstellt hat das F r und Wider einer Sanierung und eines Neubaus er rtert worden In enger Zusammenarbeit mit den Mitarbeiterinnen und Mitarbeitern der Klinik sei mit der Perspektive des Neubaus ein neues Konzept erarbeitet worden das auf einem Bezugspersonensystem f r die Patientinnen und Patienten beruhe Deshalb wurde im Beschluss des Aufsichtsrats gro er Wert darauf gelegt auch die Therapiestrukturen neben der r umlichen Verbesserung den k nftigen Erfordernissen anzupassen F r den Bauabschnitt sollen Mittel des Konjunkturpakets II und f r die folgenden Bauabschnitte Mittel nach dem Bremischen Krankenhausgesetz eingesetzt werden Die Gesundheitsbeh rde hat Mittel in H he von Mio Euro f r den ersten Bauabschnitt bereits fest zugesagt Diese Mittel m ssen bis Ende abgeflossen sein Der Umbau der bisherigen R umlichkeiten der Klinik h tte keinen nennenswerten Gewinn gebracht ist sich Grantz sicher Die Umbaukosten w rden bei der gleichen Gr enordnung liegen wie ein sparsam gebauter aber r umlich gr erer Neubau Vor allem w re f r die psychiatrische Tagesklinik und spezielle therapeutische Angebote wie Ergotherapie Bewegungstherapie sowie Gespr chsgruppen u a kein Platz Durch die jetzt beschlossene L sung w rden die Wirtschaftlichkeit gesteigert sowie die Arbeitsbedingungen f r die Mitarbeiterinnen und Mitarbeiter verbessert F r diesen Artikel wurden folgende Schlagworte vergeben Pressemitteilungen des Magistrats Disability access Disability access German Maritime Museum Leibniz Association for German Shipping History Exhibition area bridge Wolfhard Scheer Seafaring to Grasp Explore and Experience The German Maritime Museum DSM located directly on the Weser dyke presents the history of seafaring On an exhibition area of more than square meters and a park like area with large maritime objects on land and the vintage ships of the museum fleet in the Old Harbor it forms a unique ensemble of German maritime history One of the highlights is the globally unique Hanseatic cog dated The original ships in the museum harbor hundreds of valuable historical Maritime objects including ships models paintings impressive dioramas models to touch and try out inside and outside promise an entertaining as well as informative expedition through maritime history Impressions Racing yacht Diva at the entrance of the German Maritime Museum J Darlison Exhibition area Polarstation Wolfhard Scheer Exhibition area sports boats E Laska Work boats in the gravel bed Daniela Wittenberg Ocean going yacht DIVA Egbert Laska The DSM is one of the eight national research museums in Germany and a member of the Leibniz Association Aside from the permanent and special exhibitions the museum preserves among other things approx technical drawings more than photographs negatives and image files art print posters and nautical charts It s library with some titles on German maritime history and current shipping invites guests to browse through free of charge Welcome aboard The next events in our house PM Lecture Von Wohlfahrtspflege in Bremerhaven sind es insgesamt verpflichtet die soziale Arbeit f r andere oder in Selbsthilfe leisten Diese eigenst ndigen Gruppen und Verb nde repr sentieren ein breites Spektrum Prinzipien der Toleranz Offenheit und Vielfalt gibt der Parit tische als gr ter Dachverband von Selbsthilfeinitiativ im Gesundheits und Sozialbereich seinen Mitgliedsverb nden eine starke Stimme Der Parit tische und die mit ihm verbundenen Organisationen haben sich wie nur wenige andere Wohlfahrtsverb nde der Idee der sozialen Gerechtigkeit verschrieben der Chancengleichheit dem Recht eines jeden Menschen ein Leben in W rde zu f hren und seine Pers nlichkeit frei zu enthalten wie es im Grundgesetz unseres sozialen Rechtsstaats verankert ist Dieses Ziel stand bereits im Mittelpunkt als die Kreisgruppe Bremerhaven des Deutschen Parit tischen Wohlfahrtsverbands auf Initiative des einstigen Rektors und Stadthistorikers Herbert K rtge gegr ndet wurde Seit Mitte der sechziger Jahre ist mit dem damaligen DPWV das verdienstvolle Angebot des Essens auf R dern verbunden durch das seither viele Tausende von Bremerhavener Seniorinnen und Senioren ambulant mit einer warmen Mahlzeit versorgt worden sind Inzwischen betreibt der Parit tische das Essen auf R dern durch seine Tochtergesellschaft Hanse MenuService GmbH Auch mit der ambulanten Pflege und hauswirtschaftlichen Dienstleistungen die in der Tochter Parit tische Dienste Seestadt Bremerhaven organisiert sind hat sich der Verband ein wichtiges Dienstleistungsfeld er ffnet Gemeinsam mit seinen Tochtergesellschafte setzt sich der Parit tische daf r ein das Leben in Bremerhaven auch f r ltere kranke und behinderte Menschen angenehmer und menschlicher zu machen Diese Aufgabe ist gerade in Bremerhaven von besonderer Bedeutung denn wir wissen alle wie gro die sozialen Probleme in Bremerhaven sind Dazu geh ren vor allem die anhaltende Arbeitslosigkeit und die hohe Kinderarmut von rund Prozent Das soziale Gleichgewicht in unserem Land ist bedroht und deshalb brauchen wir einen Wohlfahrtsverband wie den Parit tischen der sich f r sozial Benachteiligte stark macht Der Parit tische in Bremerhaven hat sich jedoch nicht nur als sozialer Mahner sondern auch durch das b rgerschaftliche Engagement vieler ehrenamtlicher Mitarbeiterinnen und Mitarbeiter einen Namen gemacht Demokratie lebt vom Ehrenamt so lautet ein weiser und immer noch g ltiger Ausspruch unseres ersten Bundespr sidenten Theodor Heuss und dies trifft auch auf die Bremerhavenerinnen und Bremerhavener zu die unter dem Dach des Parit tischen Hilfe f r ihre Mitmenschen leisten Durch diese ehrenamtliche Arbeit die ein Kernelement einer humanen Gesellschaft und einer sozialen Demokratie ist wird unsere Stadt Bremerhaven ein gro es St ck lebenswerter Ich nehme daher dieses Jubil um gern zum Anlass allen Mitarbeiterinnen und Mitarbeitern des Parit tischen und seiner Mitgliedsverb nde im Namen der Stadt Bremerhaven f r ihren unerm dlichen Einsatz recht Wetterkontor City map City map Home Bremerhaven de Erlebnis Bremerhaven GmbH Tourism Museums Adventure Worlds Recommend page Listen Museum of the Fifties The years of the economic miracle are back Immerse yourself in the era of Elvis Presley petticoats and kidney shaped tables Hair salon from the s Erlebnis Bremerhaven GmbH The audience experiences the era of the German economic miracle very closely How did people live and work back then How did they shop How did they spend their leisure time History of mentality comes alive The museum displays typical living ensembles hallway living room kitchen bedroom children s and teenagers rooms furnishings and fittings of shops food hairdresser stationery clothing amongst others gas station office doctor s surgery as well as the Bremen pub Zum Tuschkasten The tour begins with the living conditions of the immediate post war era characterized by Notbehelf Kochkiste and hand knitted bathing suit Topics of social history are documented in display cases for example the orientation towards America love of Venice and Paris design fashion party and travel culture sex roles the bringing up of children and many other subjects The museum which has been furnished with extensive textual material in collaboration with Bremen university concerns itself with the ambience of the life during that period including the Gro en Schweigen in the Helmut Gross The Seaside City of Bremerhaven is located where the waters of the River Weser flow into the North Sea Bremerhaven the largest city on the German North Sea Coast is framed by the ocean and the charming outskirts Rows of lighthouses along the River Weser museum ships sway in the harbors in the German Maritime Museum the world s oldest cog is anchored windjammers and ocean giants take course for our seaside city In the Shop Window Fishery Harbor the smell of freshly smoked fish is in the air Stop by and visit the new theme exhibition Expedition Northern Seas where you can dive into underwater worlds and in the Sea Fish Cooking Studio fish gourmets will definitely get their fill From here you can take a tour with the HarborBus through Europe s largest container and automobile transshipment hub an exciting experience for all ages In the Havenwelten Bremerhaven the Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost the German Emigration Center Bremerhaven as well as the Zoo at the Sea with the North Sea Aquarium are waiting to be discovered If you like to shop the pedestrian zone the indoor Columbus Shopping Center and the Mediterraneo all invite you to an enjoyable shopping spree In the award winning Historical Museum Bremerhaven the history of our city is told in an entertaining and informative manner Extraordinary adventures await our guests in Bremerhaven Discover our Seaside City and its outskirts on your own and utilize the available possibilities Well known and popular international national and regional cycle routes travel through our seaside city Such as the River Weser cycle route Its wide variety of landscapes and scenic beauty can hardly be surpassed and a visit to Bremerhaven is always well worth a stop The Fisch und Schipp Route leads along the harbor basins ships and fish are guaranteed With our nature route Wasser Wind und Wiesen you will get to know our seaside city from a completely different side Cyclist friendly accommodations well signed routes in the city and the green outskirts lead you directly to our attractions and highlights And on top our cycle stations in the Shop Window Fishery Harbor and in the Havenwelten Bremerhaven offer you full service ranging from rentals to repairs baggage storage as well as touristic information We look forward to greet you Es konnten keine Koordinaten ermittelt werden Klicken Sie hier um den Standort manuell zu ermitteln Position bernehmen You can find us here RadStation Schaufenster Fischereihafen Am Schaufenster Bremerhaven Go to city map Contact Address RadStation Schaufenster Fischereihafen Am Organization Event area around the New Harbor Mailin Knoke Lots of windjammers to look and feel along with a colorful program in the Havenwelten Bremerhaven on land and at sea are the exciting ingredients of the new big maritime event Seaside City Festival Shore Leave Bremerhaven which will take place for the third time in Bremerhaven from May th th The Seaside City s retail partners will also participate in this event with Sunday shopping Original acrobats street food and maritime crafts can also be enjoyed and experienced A diverse music program as well as lots of activities for children complement the eventful festival days Yet the real stars of this event are the big and small ships under sails or motorized A hearty welcome to the Seaside City of Bremerhaven Magazine Recommend page Listen Schippertage Bremerhaven from th to th August Traditional mud flat sail ships from Germany and the Netherlands are headed for the second time towards Bremerhaven Mooring of ships in the Old Harbor Mailin Knoke Aaken Bojer Ewer Galioten Kuffen and Tjalken were the most important way of transportation in the first decades of the th century They were mostly used at the German and Dutch coasts Today the freighters with a flat keel and chunky bow are a special class of traditional ships A handful of flat bottomed ships can always be found in Bremerhaven but for the Schippertage additional ships from the Netherlands and East Frisia will arrive A joint run into port into the Old Harbor is planned for Friday around pm and a highlight for all ship lovers Furthermore there will be a maritime program on Saturday and Sunday craftsman will take you on a journey back in time with their historical work Shanty Choirs will perform live on stage You ll also have the chance to have a little chit chat with the skippers while enjoying a nice cup of coffee On both days food and beverages will be available around the Old Harbor The event is held in cooperation with the Schiffergilde Bremerhaven e V and the German Maritime Museum Leibniz Institute for German Maritime History Participating ships The Mien Wicht from Drakenburg Germany Oliver Seidler The Tjalk Anna Marie was built around in Groningen The ship is equipped with two engines Mailin Knoke The Date built around belongs to the group of Zeeschouwen which is known as gaffel decked flat bottomed vessels which originate in the fishing on the Zuiderzee and the adjacent Wattengebiet Mailin Knoke The Zeeschouw is a proven Dutch flat bottom ship It is suitable with a mast laying device not only for trips to the North Sea and Baltic Sea the IJsselmeer and the Wattenmeeren but also for Oder Elbe Weser Ems Mailin Knoke The Lemster Aak Theepot was built in the Netherlands in the s of the last century The rented steel ship s body was rebuilt at the Boomsma shipyard in Sneek Friesland province in Mailin Knoke At the beginning of the th century the Tjalk Wappen von Ihlow was built in Groningen It was one of the first to be built with an iron hull Mailin Knoke The Klipperaak Vrouwe Elisabeth from the Netherlands Wiebe Brienen Es konnten keine Koordinaten ermittelt werden Klicken Sie hier um den Standort manuell zu Bremerhaven grows by the sea The architecture is courageos the subjects revolutionary View from the wharf to the Harbor Worlds Helmut Gross The Seaside City is opening up a new chapter in its history The Havenwelten Bremerhaven Harbor Worlds Bremerhaven are being built in the city at the River Weser dyke At present it is still the largest municipal construction project on the North Sea coast but it will soon be a maritime tourism resort with unique attractions Climate House Bremerhaven East Atlantic Hotel Sail City with the look out platform Mediterraneo Lloyd Marina and living at the dyke Not to mention the successful German Emigration Center the Zoo at the Sea the German Maritime Museum the submarine Wilhelm Bauer and the Historical Museum Bremerhaven The building of the Havenwelten Bremerhaven has already visibly altered the center of Bremerhaven But the Seaside City skyline of tomorrow will be even more spectacular You can see this for yourself Check out the Havenwelten Bremerhaven and look forward to fascinating experiences in the Seaside City of Bremerhaven Impressions Exterior view of the Climate House Bremerhaven Ost Jens Rilke Exterior view of the German Emigration Center Kay Riechers Polar bear Lloyd in the Zoo at the Sea Zoo am Meer Entrance of the German Maritime Museum J Darlison Exterior view of the Historical Museum Bremerhaven Historisches Museum Bremerhaven Now the mega project with all its facilities is completed Almost a million additional tourists will discover the seaside city from a new and most spectacular aspect Guided Tours Listen Zoo at the Sea with the North Sea Aquarium An experience for young and old Eye to eye with polar bears seals penguins etc On land with a view of the ocean or through huge underwater windows Underwater shot of a polar bear Zoo am Meer The visitors of the Zoo at the Sea get an impression of the habitat of polar bears polar foxes common seals fur seals and penguins bizarre barren deserts of ice colourful tundra landscapes framed by water and more water Views to the river Weser frequently provide an impression of the immense vastness of the landscapes represented Underwater views open entirely different dimensions flying penguins diving polar bears and majestically gliding seals As a contrast to this there are also monkeys who due to the tradition of seafaring in Bremerhaven seamen brought them to the city from their foreign travels also must have their place in the new zoo Thus chimpanzees roam the tropical jungle and savannah landscaped on the search for something to eat and poke an artificial termite hill for delicacies Impressions Aerial view from the Zoo at the Sea Zoo am Meer Gannets under water Zoo am Meer Young Chimpanzee Zoo am Meer Penguins under water Zoo am Meer Polar bear Lloyd Zoo am Meer Penguins at feeding time Zoo am Meer Monkeys playing with a food container Zoo am Meer Impressive seals basking in a near natural grounds Zoo am Meer Ein Pinguin unter Wasser Zoo am Meer Puma cat Mingo patrolling its territorial boundaries Zoo am Meer Children have the chance to playfully compete with the skills of the animals on parallel adventure trails or to explore the small adventure playground To conclude a visit to the zoo the visitor can relax on the terrace with a cup of coffee and enjoy the endless expanse of the ocean not an everyday view Additional highlights are the animal feedings and the seal training In the nine North Sea aquariums with a total water volume of about liters you can see under water life from various habitats of the North Sea Fish from the brackish water from the Weser such as pike eel or sea trout are presented In seagrass beds the young fish pipefish and sea horses can be observed The reconstruction of a harbor mole with its inhabitants as well as the thickets of seaweed in front of Helgioland are surely impressive Dive into the underwater world of the new North Sea Aquarium in the Zoo at the Sea with us Es department Historisches Museum Bremerhaven Situated on the river Geeste the award winning Historisches Museum Bremerhaven presents history art and culture of Bremerhaven and its region In the exhibition halls of sqm visitors can make an exciting journey through time that reaches from the earliest traces of human beings in the Elbe Weser triangle to a cinema from the ies A complete historical shipyard with a shipbuilding place and a shipyard workers house scenes from dock labour a walk in harbor pub a fishmonger s shop or a machine hall with operable steam and refrigeration machines from ice production are just a few examples of the manifold living and working environment at the museum Impressions A look over the shoulder of Admiral Brommy in the light filled permanent exhibition of the Historical Museum Bremerhaven Historisches Museum Bremerhaven In historical fishmonger the entire range is offered Historisches Museum Bremerhaven An American military Jeep symbolizes the time of Bremerhaven as American occupation zone after World War II Historisches Museum Bremerhaven On the upstairs gallery various exhibitions are held regularly Historisches Museum Rental Service Bremerhaven de Kay Riechers Tourism Museums Adventure Worlds Recommend page Listen Disability access Disability access German Emigration Center Bremerhaven An exciting journey through years of emigration and immigration history Aboard an Ocean Liner in Stefan Volk Waiting on the wharf waving good bye from the gangway then the journey starts For more than seven million emigrants who left from Bremerhaven between on their journey to the New World this is the moment of departure For the visitors of the German Emigration Center this is the start of their travel through years of German migration history Located on that very harbor where the emigrant ships departed you will now find the awarded theme museum in which vistors follow the personal path of an emigrant from the time of departure to the conditions experienced during the crossing up until the arrival in the New World After emigrating to the New World visitors immigrate to Germany In a reconstructed shopping mall of the year the year the Federal Republic of Germany enacted a recruitment Stopp for foreign workerk visitors trace the footsteps of immigrants such as Huguenots Guest Workers or Syrian civil war refugees Impressions Exterior view Stefan Volk At the docks Stefan Volk Onboard a sailing ship in Stefan Volk Onboard an ocean steamer in Stefan Volk Gallery of the million Stefan Volk Entry in the USA Stefan Volk Ellis Island in New York Stefan Volk Restaurant Speisesaal Steak Fish in the German Emigration Center Stefan Volk Quay of tears in the German Emigration Center Stefan Volk Grand Central Terminal Ilka Seer Shopping arcade in the German Emigration Center Kay Riechers At the end of the tour visitors have the opportunity to embark on a personal search for their own ancestors in two international databases Aside from the permanent exhibition changing special exhibitions events and seminars deal more closely with various aspects of migration The next events in our house AM Touristenattraktion Klimahaus schon jetzt ein Gl cksfall Bremerhaven de SAIL Bremerhaven Evening mood in the New Harbor Previous Stop or Start Next Helmut Gross Sail In Thousands of visitors admire the ship s parade from the dyke Previous Stop or Start Next Helmut Gross Sailors move Through the inner city to the Theodor Heuss Place Previous Stop or Start Next Helmut Gross Flag parade Morning flag parade at the New Harbor Previous Stop or Start Next Helmut Gross Recommend page Listen Welcome to the SAIL Bremerhaven The International Windjammer Festival from th rd August SAIL Programm Service Contact Logo of the SAIL Bremerhaven Erlebnis Bremerhaven GmbH Sail Bremerhaven has long become an international institution in a city and region that is traditionally and historically closely connected with ships and sail More than great ocean going sailing vessels were built between and at the Rickmers and the Joh C Tecklenborg shipyards And the great sail training ships like the Kruzenshtern formerly the Padua or the Statsraad Lehmkuhl formerly the Grossherzog Friedrich August are still sailing nowadays Not to mention the barque Alexander von Humboldt II which has been Bremerhaven s ambassador afloat in the international community of the tall ships and sail training since But Sail Bremerhaven is also and above all an expression of the identity of the greatest city on the German North Sea Coast which has drawn its existence for more than years from shipbuilding nautical trading and the commerce generated by its harbor The exploration of the seas and the poles of our Earth the research into the German and European nautical history or the authentic preservation of the cultural maritime inheritance also nowadays belong to the great tasks of the city which is now for the tenth time since the host for the International Windjammer Festival Sail Bremerhaven And it is a good tradition that on the th rd August the government of the Federal Republic of Germany and of the State of Bremen together with the City of Bremerhaven on their part again invite the international community of sailing people on the large and small windjammers on the ocean going yachts and on the tradition rich ships to the seaport of Bremerhaven a city that has made great changes in its appearance in the past years and has developed into a maritime center for research high technology culture and maritime tourism Welcome to Bremerhaven Es konnten keine Koordinaten ermittelt werden Klicken Sie hier um den Standort manuell zu ermitteln Position bernehmen You can find us here Erlebnis Christensen und Herr Professor Obrant Universit tsklinikum Lund unterzeichnet Professor Per Odin Hauptziel dieser Vereinbarung ist eine noch bessere Patientenversorgung und eine intensive Zusammenarbeit in den Bereichen Ausbildung und Forschung Dies soll durch Austausch von Informationen Methoden und Personal m glich werden Diese Kooperation wird von Professor Per Odin der ab zus tzlich zu der Leitung der Neurologischen Klinik im Klinikum Bremerhaven Reinkenheide eine Teilzeitforschungspr in Lund angenommen hat koordiniert werden Das erste Gebiet in der sich die Kooperation sich die Kooperationspartner deutlich qualit tserh hende Effekte vor allem in der Patientenversorgung aber auch in der klinischen Forschung im Klinikum Bremerhaven Reinkenheide Die Stadt Lund liegt in S dschweden etwa km von Kopenhagen entfernt Das Krankenhaus in Lund ist eines von Schwedens sechs Universit tskrankenh usern und hat ein Aufnahmegebiet von Millionen Einwohnern Das Universit tskrankenhaus Lund hat Angestellte davon rzte Es gibt Betten und jedes Jahr werden ca Arztbesuche und Operationen durchgef hrt Neurowissenschaftlic geh rt Lund weltweit zu den produktivsten Zahlenwerk bietet den Mietparteien eine Orientierungsm glichkeit um die Miete nach Art Gr e Ausstattung Beschaffenheit und Lage der Wohnung zu vereinbaren erl utert der Vorsitzende des Gutachterausschusses f r Grundst ckswerte und Leiter des Vermessungs und Katasteramts Ulrich Gellhaus Die Angaben im Mietrahmen sind Erfahrungswerte der vergangenen vier Jahre f r den Raum Bremerhaven nach dem Stand von Ende Nach den derzeit stagnierenden Mieten sieht Gellhaus eine neue Entwicklung durch die Aufwertung von Wohnungen K nftig w rden barrierefreie also rollstuhlgerechte Umbauten und die Modernisierung nach der Energieeinsparverord EnEV st rker zu Buche schlagen Der Mietspiegel wird gemeinsam erarbeitet und herausgegeben vom Mieterverein Haus und Grund dem Ring Deutscher Makler und von der Gesch ftsstelle des Gutachterausschusses f r Grundst ckswerte Das Zahlenwerk kann als pdf Datei unter www gutachterausschuss bremerhaven de und bei den beteiligten Vereinen heruntergeladen Bremerhaven Google Soziale Medien Bremerhaven de Laurence Delderfield Tourism Museums Adventure Worlds Recommend page Listen Climate House Bremerhaven East Climate journey around the world Be amazed sweat and freeze in the Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost Exhibition area Kamarun Laurence Delderfield Take a trip round the world and experience the world s climate zones From the refreshing coolness on the alp in Switzerland through the scorching heat of the Sahel to the iciness of the Antarctic as well as the heavenly climate of the South Seas and the unsettled weather in Northern Germany On the Journey in the Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost visitors can experience first hand how the people live in the Earth s most important climate zones The tour along the eighth degree of longitude East leads through sceneries that are built true to original locations Impressions Exhibition area Alaska Laurence Delderfield Exhibition area atmosphere Laurence Delderfield Exterior view of the Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost Laurence Delderfield Exhibition area Samoa Laurence Delderfield Exhibition area Antarctica Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost Entrance area Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost Exhibition area prospects Klimahaus Bremerhaven Ost The Perspectives is another major section of the exhibition which takes a look at past and present climates and the impacts on the future In the section Opportunities the visitor is shown choices of action he can for example test hands on in theme chambers how he can contribute personally in everyday life to the reduction in CO emissions The Bremerhaven de Kay Riechers Tourism Museums Adventure Worlds Recommend page Listen Museums Adventure Worlds Museums adventure worlds and culture invite you to discover Not only small museums await you however true adventure worlds For example feel the climate along the th degree of longitude and explore the various climate zones Or authentically experience European emigration and immigration history in the German Emigration Center Take an extraordinary journey through time in the Historical Museum Are you interested in maritime topics Then you should visit the German Maritime Museum with the famous Hansekogge An experience for young and old is certainly the Zoo at the Sea with the North Sea Aquarium Here you can marvel polar bears seals penguins barnacles and others In the Shop WIndow Fishery Harbor you will find the Expedition Northern Seas which gives you an insight into the habitats of the fish from the North Sea Bremerhaven s cultural is rich so that art lovers will naturally also get their fill ranging from historical masterpieces to modern installations you can surely discover specialties We look forward to greet you Keyword Search Select one or more filters Attraction
